name:X‚Äçu‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçx‚Äçu‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçd‚Äçe‚Äçm‚Äçe‚Äçi‚Äçs‚Äçh‚Äçi‚Äçz‚Äçh‚Äçi‚Äçl‚Äçv
info:Superior Sea-view Queen Room
info:Stayed in February 2024
info:Family
info:18 Reviews
rating:4.2
posted:Posted February 29, 2024
msg:It takes less than three hours to drive from Chongzuo to Beihai Shangri-La. There are many hotels in Beihai. It took me a long time to choose this hotel. Parking is convenient. The ground parking lot is large. The concierge at the door is very polite. He helps with luggage and opens the door. Recommended travel routes...
There was a huge queue for check-in after 14:00, and I waited for a long time. When checking in, I was told that all three rooms were being cleaned and that I would have to wait for more than an hour. I took my baby to the nearby Ancient Weapons Museum. I got free tickets but also needed an ID card to enter. After looking at it and not being interested, I went back to the hotel and ordered a fried rice set for my baby at the lobby bar. It took half an hour for this to be served. About two hours later, the room had not been cleaned yet, so I was finally given one to rest first.
When I looked at the room, it was indeed a bit old. The curtains are manually operated, and the TV is very small, with limited definition and cannot be projected onto the screen. The bathroom is not separated from dry and wet areas. Standing in the bathtub to take a shower is really nostalgic. The air conditioning control is still manually adjusted... The large floor-to-ceiling windows are okay. There is a seaside trestle downstairs. The temperature in the room is also good. I called to ask for a fence. It was delivered quickly. The window of the room needs to be signed by an exempted attendant to get the key to open it.
After dinner, I came back to get the room cards for the other two rooms. When I came up, one of them couldn't be opened. I called and told me that I had to go to the front desk to get it. It was too much trouble. I went down and said there was a problem with the system, and asked the waiter to open the door for me. There were still many people checking in at night.
The wind was too strong and the temperature dropped the next day. I didn't dare to let the baby go out because he had a slight cold, so he stayed in the hotel. There is a fitness center on B1. As soon as you go there, you will see the children's activity center. It is open for one hour in the morning and one hour in the afternoon every day. You can do crafts for a fee. In my impression, Shangri-La has always done a good job in children's activities. There is neither a children's paradise nor a wider selection of children's activities. There is only one Lego board in the room. If you play here, it will cost 298 a day. I am really dumbfounded. Just one Lego is so expensive...
Regarding breakfast, there was a long queue on the first day and it was hard to find a seat. You have to queue for a while to eat noodles, there are people everywhere, and the meal replenishment is slow. There were relatively few people on the second day. I had pork trotter noodles and Chongqing noodles, which tasted good. There are also Vietnamese roll noodles, shrimp cakes and other special snacks. There are a wide variety of fruit drinks, and there are relatively few stir-fried and steamed foods.
Overall, the facilities are old, the service is good, and the room temperature is very good. The breakfast experience is quite good if there are not many people. Old five-star hotels should develop more entertainment projects and parent-child activities in resort cities. After staying for three days, I was indeed a bit disappointed.

name:S‚Äçi‚Äçl‚Äçe‚Äçn‚Äçc‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçk‚Äçy‚Äçs

posted:Posted May 13, 2023
msg:It is said that "live in the new but not the old", but in fact, I do not reject old hotels. Many hotels that have been open for a long time have old facilities, but the location will be better, the management team and service will be more meticulous, and the comprehensive attributes will not Difference.
.
This time I stayed at Shangri-La Hotel, Beihai. This is one of the first batch of five-star hotels in China. It has been in operation for nearly 30 years, so the location is very good, with a sea view. The attractions are also only 2 kilometers away.
.
The building of the hotel is not too high, only 17 floors. The exterior is still the old-school classic white square design of Shangri-La. This time, I directly booked an executive suite. After arriving at the hotel, the front desk took the initiative to upgrade to a luxury suite on the highest 16th floor. Although the area is the same, the view is sure. Even better, the hotel mascot chef Xiaogui was given as a gift, which left a good impression on me at the beginning, and the Horizon Club Sea View Room I booked the next day did not ask me to change rooms, and I continued to live in a suite. I like it.
.
The luxury suite is nominally 77 square meters, and the actual body feels larger than some of the current 90+ standard rooms. It is a corner room with two sides of the landscape, and the house type is relatively square. It is more spacious, the living room has a dining table for four, a sofa set for guests, and an extra bed by the window? I was wondering about this at first, because I didn't ask for an extra bed and didn't need an extra bed, but later I found that it was quite comfortable to lie on it and watch the sea while swiping my phone.
.
A rich fruit plate and snacks have been prepared, including dried jackfruit and sesame cod granules. Although the facilities are very old, they are well maintained, and the carpets and sofas are not obviously dirty.
.
In the minibar, the kettle has already boiled the water and keeps it warm. It is really considerate in the rainy weather, and the 5 tea bags exclusive to Shangri-La are stuffed so hard that they can‚Äôt fit. The free water is pure water.
.
The bedroom is very spacious. It‚Äôs a pity that there is no stool at the end of the bed. There is a sofa and a desk by the window. It‚Äôs troublesome to switch the lights without a master control. This old hotel can‚Äôt help. For this book, there is a turndown service, and a bookmark of Lost Horizon and a stewed good night sugar water will be given away.
.
The space in the master bathroom is relatively compact, with double washbasins, the toilet and the washbasin are put together, and the shower is still an old design that fits into the bathtub without any changes. You can only stand in the bathtub to shower, but the bathtub is relatively short, so it‚Äôs okay to get in and out It is convenient and will put a non-slip mat inside. I like L'Occitane's jasmine series for spare parts, but only 2 sets are limited per day.
.
Equipped with two types of bathrobes, thick and thin, the thin one is very beautiful and has a sense of vacation. It is very avant-garde to have a design close to floor-to-ceiling windows in the 1990s. Unfortunately, there is no balcony. The sea view and trestle outside the window are really invincible, although it is rainy But the ebb and flow of the tide is very obvious. It is also an interesting sight to see many fishermen wading in the shallows to catch the sea every day.
.
Generally speaking, although the style and facilities are old and the bathroom feels poor, the service and landscape are excellent, and the feeling of living is still good.

If it is said that Beihai is cloudy and sunny in the morning, and the afternoon is as warm as early spring, the heating in the hotel is 100% full, and the short-sleeved hotel in the hotel is short-sleeved, and you may be forced to go back to the room and add clothes when you go out, hahahahahaha.

msg:Originally planned to check out early, change hotels, + complain. The manager handled it well. Praise it.
I came to Beihai from Beijing for a business trip. I originally planned to stay for three days. People in the north feel that it is a bit cold at night. I am used to being warm at home at night. On the day I checked in, I asked why the warm air was not warm. The waiter told me that it will be warmer later. After waiting for several hours, there was still no warm air, and I didn‚Äôt take a shower to sleep because of the cold. I reported this the next day, and the waiter told me to let the engineering repair it for me, so I went out to do errands. No one paid attention to me all day. I went back to the hotel room at 6:00 pm. It was still cold. I went downstairs to inquire and met the lobby manager. I was told that I had just asked about the project. exploded. The co-author except the lobby manager is fooling me, knowing that I wouldn't live here without warm air.
The first thing the lobby manager did was send an electric heater to my room, and at the same time told me that the project had been notified to turn on the heater. Then, seeing that I was not satisfied, he changed the room for me. This time, there was an independent cabinet in the room. The air conditioner and the room are bigger. Anyway, it calmed me down and I stopped complaining.
In general, the staff at Shangri-La should be trained on how to deal with problems. It‚Äôs not enough to deal with them. They should consider the reputation of the hotel. A manager is a manager. Waiters should think about why they can be managers. Learn more from others.

We booked the Shangri-La Hotel in Beihai for one night, and took a boat to Weizhou Island the next day. As a result, the ticket was cancelled due to the typhoon. The room was tight during the peak travel period. We wanted a lot of rooms without pre-booking. The line was big and small, and there was a lot of luggage. At that time, the itinerary was all disrupted. I was very anxious at the front desk and repeatedly asked the staff who received me to help us solve it. She continued to live, she worked tirelessly to help us figure out how to solve the problem, while she kept comforting us and told us where there were delicious and fun things. She smiled and faced us from beginning to end until she finally helped us solve the problem, although Wearing a mask, we feel your beauty and warmth as well. You are the pride of Shangri-La Hotel! Because you will always choose Shangri-La Hotel in the future, (we know her name is Wu Min through other staff) Thank you! Highly recommend Beihai Shangri-La, rich breakfast, delicious Shang Palace, the most humane swimming pool open from 8 in the morning to 11 in the evening.
